) AS a0

    SELECT e."Id", e."Address", e."CategoryId", e."City", e."Context", e."CreatorEmail", e."Date", e."Description", e."Imageurl", e."IsCancelled", e."Price", e."Ticketcount", e."Title", t."Id" AS "Id0", t."BookingDate", t."CustomerEmail", t."EventId", t."IsCancelled" AS "IsCancelled0", t."Quantity", t."Total"
